using \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a6dc28d0ec823c5116db403b47a6770c0}{i}} = j) \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1f8ac598ec2e995f720ab41e50da1de6}{until}} \{ Given \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} replacement \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}} are zero \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}}, we could simply create them without ever looking at \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} original blocks. Sadly \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} creation of zero \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}} turns out to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} slightly more painful than one would wish \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_adfe6b2bdd05330e241df296c09b1de2a}{because}} they have to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} created as \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}}(possibly distributed) \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} C\+R\+Double\+Matrix. The relevant code is contained \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} source code but we won \textquotesingle{}t discuss it here since \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} more common situation is one where we actually want to modify \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} already existing entries of an already existing block matrix. Therefore we simply extract \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} set its initially nonzero entries to zero(admittedly \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} bit silly -\/-\/ we now have \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} sparse matrix full of zeroes, but it \textquotesingle{}s just \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} demonstration!)\+:\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1f8ac598ec2e995f720ab41e50da1de6}{until}} this is just an example! We then pass \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \textbackslash{}skip loop of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a6dc28d0ec823c5116db403b47a6770c0}{i}} The rest of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} coarse\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+one Coarsening/combining \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} N\+EW F\+E\+A\+T\+U\+R\+E\+S\+:\+How to coarsen/combine \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} for use by subsidiary block preconditioners. \textbackslash{}subsubsection coarse\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+one\+\_\+theory Theory In \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a8827906ff74d898ef20bb0e9605e7e65}{examples}} presented so far we have demonstrated how to combine various \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} into compound \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ab2797c2e731d57d96d8dec396dd3f47d}{order}} to facilitate \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} application of certain preconditioning operations. For \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acdb7a40a5c0efe5eff5bb57ba88d5b24}{instance}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} many of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} previous \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a8827906ff74d898ef20bb0e9605e7e65}{examples}} we performed \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2dd5f13c53edb190f5451684014eed5c}{vector}} product using \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} compound matrix \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aeb67b16f41be1903f840dc845012c7ec}{B\+\_\+}}\{12\} \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} was(formally) formed by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} concatenation of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} 2x3 \char`\"{}top right\char`\"{} off-\/diagonal \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/sized system. We also showed how subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2edeca293cddae778e715dea443cfdc9}{preconditioners}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} operate on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} specific number of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} instructed to operate on selected \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} from \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/sized system. Our standard \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aee0b46a7944d413c53157110d1f7f4d7}{example}} for this was \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} 2D Navier-\/Stokes \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} operates on three \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}}(two fluid \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a200481dd99050de703e95310b8d7188a}{velocities}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} one \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a622e9a161fe300e2ba2f734430187e19}{pressure}}) \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} is used as \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} an F\+SI \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_abc882676ce6535f83eef31e4c8889d44}{problem}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} also involves additional \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aea1877bbfb3f4a1f7d7c64edba58d5f5}{dofs}} associated \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid mechanics(e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} two solid displacement components). This was done by informing \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/sized system to regard as \char`\"{}its own\char`\"{} when calling its \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} turn\+\_\+into\+\_\+subsidiary\+\_\+block\+\_\+preconditioner(...) function. This implies \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} remains unaware of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7005143667a7d93ac15567de99c9459d}{any}} compound \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} may have been formed \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} its master preconditioner. The functionality presented so far only allows us to associate \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary block preconditioner. It is therefore not possible(without further functionality \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} we explain \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} this \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aee0b46a7944d413c53157110d1f7f4d7}{example}}) to use \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} if \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} are \char`\"{}too fine-\/grained\char`\"{}. This arises, for \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acdb7a40a5c0efe5eff5bb57ba88d5b24}{instance}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} Navier-\/Stokes \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a585197cbf62aba1f1ec0bbb2b5c4c0c9}{problems}} where \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} sub-\/divides \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} two components of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} fluid velocity into degrees of freedom on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} domain boundary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} those \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} interior. It is then necessary to make \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} act on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} combined \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} process \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} we describe as \char`\"{}coarsening\char`\"{}. We illustrate \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} procedure by returning, yet again, to our 5x5 block linear system \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} we wish to precondition \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ae5d3b6fe51905f59612f7a9bf14caea4}{f}} bf \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1588f3a894c121120972cf2a5b4c9ac3}{z}} etc Within \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} given \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} such derived \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}} are typically pre computed by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} s \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} this approach does not work if \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} modified block is to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} used \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} as discussed \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} previous by default \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} will extract its block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}} directly from \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full size system matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} will therefore ignore \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7005143667a7d93ac15567de99c9459d}{any}} (local) modifications made by its master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}}(s). What is therefore required is \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aed55b92e2cd68f214bea36d34e07fc08}{method}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} indicates to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} block preconditioning framework \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} given sub-\/block is not to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} extracted from \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full system matrix but to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} represented by suitable replacement matrix. We demonstrate this methodology by re-\/visiting \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} considered \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} previous \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aee0b46a7944d413c53157110d1f7f4d7}{example}}

\item 
Next we set up \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary operators required by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} We start \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}}(\textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}tilde S\textbackslash{}f\$). We extract \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid matrix block \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ae5d3b6fe51905f59612f7a9bf14caea4}{f}} \$S\textbackslash{}f\$ from \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} Jacobian using \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} Block\+Preconditioner \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aed55b92e2cd68f214bea36d34e07fc08}{method}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} get\+\_\+block(...) \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} then set up \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} Note compared to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} previous we have used an pointer \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aaf4e33e2bac366e56327e2c241ad0c39}{based}} version of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a115e3d779dcec89667c9b94b99e95f86}{get\+\_\+block}} (...) function. \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a193d0baa9ebd9824d79e8e7a441aea18}{However}}
\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} extracted block can \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} deleted since \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2dd5f13c53edb190f5451684014eed5c}{vector}} product \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a18de562496954a7a75e14741e969012d}{operator retains the relevant data. The F\+S\+I preconditioner is now ready to be used. \textbackslash{}subsection solve Preconditioner Solve The \textbackslash{}c preconditioner\+\_\+solve}} (...) \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aed55b92e2cd68f214bea36d34e07fc08}{method}} applies \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} input \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2dd5f13c53edb190f5451684014eed5c}{vector}} \textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}bf y\textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} returns \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} result \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}bf z\textbackslash{}f\$. We start by applying \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} Navier-\/Stokes \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}tilde F\textbackslash{}f\$ to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} fluid \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ac3c3773dbb42cd2b6dfda4f2743e797e}{elements}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} y\+\_\+f of \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} y. Since \textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}tilde F\textbackslash{}f\$ is \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} we apply it to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/length \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a8eaf6a27a1ad9459eb051d39b708b2c4}{y}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1588f3a894c121120972cf2a5b4c9ac3}{z}} vectors \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} contain both \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} fluid \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} solid unknowns. mainpage oomph lib s Block Preconditioning Framework \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} oomph lib s block preconditioning framework provides an environment for \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} development of block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2edeca293cddae778e715dea443cfdc9}{preconditioners}} for \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} iterative solution of linear systems by Krylov subspace methods The framework is \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aaf4e33e2bac366e56327e2c241ad0c39}{based}} on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a12586199f621293656e6a34caf0a072e}{classification}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_abc882676ce6535f83eef31e4c8889d44}{problem}} s \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} multi physics typically \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aeef45233f4d17b9819e1856bb579fcf7}{represent}} different physical quantities A key feature of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} framework is \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} it allows existing block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} hierarchical \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2edeca293cddae778e715dea443cfdc9}{preconditioners}} for related multi physics \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a585197cbf62aba1f1ec0bbb2b5c4c0c9}{problems}} This means \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} existing Navier Stokes \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} etc n n b Role b of b \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} block preconditioning framework visits all \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ac3c3773dbb42cd2b6dfda4f2743e797e}{elements}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} make contributions to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} Jacobian matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} associates \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} global equation number of each \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} type specified by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} element The block preconditioning framework is given access to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ac3c3773dbb42cd2b6dfda4f2743e797e}{elements}} each of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} is assumed to contain \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ac3c3773dbb42cd2b6dfda4f2743e797e}{elements}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a488342c731882ee60a1223b02fe1b777}{single}} type The total number of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} Next we set up \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary operators required by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} We start \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}}(\textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}tilde S\textbackslash{}f\$). We extract \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid matrix block \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ae5d3b6fe51905f59612f7a9bf14caea4}{f}} \$S\textbackslash{}f\$ from \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} Jacobian using \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} Block\+Preconditioner \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aed55b92e2cd68f214bea36d34e07fc08}{method}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a115e3d779dcec89667c9b94b99e95f86}{get\+\_\+block}}(...) \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} then set up \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} Note \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a3c8ce4610088ab0019d3e1fc8c85fe12}{that}}
\item 
Next we set up \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary operators required by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} We start \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}}(\textbackslash{}f\$\textbackslash{}tilde S\textbackslash{}f\$). {\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a6dc28d0ec823c5116db403b47a6770c0}{i}} =  j) \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1f8ac598ec2e995f720ab41e50da1de6}{until}} \{ Given \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} replacement \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}} are zero \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}}, we could simply create them without ever looking at \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} original blocks. Sadly \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} creation of zero \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a484447fc0413c753fa95dcff66bc063b}{matrices}} turns out to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} slightly more painful than one would wish \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_adfe6b2bdd05330e241df296c09b1de2a}{because}} they have to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} created as \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} (possibly distributed) \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} C\+R\+Double\+Matrix. The relevant code is contained \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} source code but we won\textquotesingle{}t discuss it here since \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} more common situation is one where we actually want to modify \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} already existing entries of an already existing block matrix. Therefore we simply extract \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} set its initially nonzero entries to zero (admittedly \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} bit silly -\/-\/ we now have \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} sparse matrix full of zeroes, but it\textquotesingle{}s just \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} demonstration!)\+: \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1f8ac598ec2e995f720ab41e50da1de6}{until}} this is just an example! \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} off diagonal mat vec operators\+: \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1f8ac598ec2e995f720ab41e50da1de6}{until}} \} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1f8ac598ec2e995f720ab41e50da1de6}{until}} \} \textbackslash{}subsubsection two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+three\+\_\+upper\+\_\+triangular\+\_\+with\+\_\+replace\+\_\+solve The preconditioner\+\_\+solve() function The \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} preconditioner\+\_\+solve() function is completely identical to \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} one used \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} previous \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}}, so we omit \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} code listing -\/-\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2edeca293cddae778e715dea443cfdc9}{preconditioners}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2dd5f13c53edb190f5451684014eed5c}{vector}} product operator work \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} same way but now simply operate on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} replacement \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} where they have been set. \textbackslash{}subsubsection two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+three\+\_\+upper\+\_\+triangular\+\_\+with\+\_\+replace\+\_\+clean The \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a5be663dc283b34c92f797a040c305562}{clean\+\_\+up\+\_\+my\+\_\+memory}}() function Memory is cleaned up as \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a57ad40a9de7c2a027446e1e0b32aa678}{before}}, so we omit \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} code listing. \#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\#\# coarse\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+one Coarsening/combining \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} N\+EW F\+E\+A\+T\+U\+R\+E\+S\+: How to coarsen/combine \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} for use by subsidiary block preconditioners. \textbackslash{}subsubsection coarse\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+two\+\_\+plus\+\_\+one\+\_\+theory Theory In \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a8827906ff74d898ef20bb0e9605e7e65}{examples}} presented so far we have demonstrated how to combine various \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} into compound \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ab2797c2e731d57d96d8dec396dd3f47d}{order}} to facilitate \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} application of certain preconditioning operations. For \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acdb7a40a5c0efe5eff5bb57ba88d5b24}{instance}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} many of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} previous \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a8827906ff74d898ef20bb0e9605e7e65}{examples}} we performed \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} matrix \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2dd5f13c53edb190f5451684014eed5c}{vector}} product using \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} compound matrix \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aeb67b16f41be1903f840dc845012c7ec}{B\+\_\+}}\{12\} \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} was (formally) formed by \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} concatenation of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} 2x3 \char`\"{}top right\char`\"{} off-\/diagonal \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/sized system. We also showed how subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2edeca293cddae778e715dea443cfdc9}{preconditioners}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} operate on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} specific number of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} can \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a52086336de840f7dda01f56e7d1cf1ed}{be}} instructed to operate on selected \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} from \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/sized system. Our standard \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aee0b46a7944d413c53157110d1f7f4d7}{example}} for this was \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} 2D Navier-\/Stokes \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} operates on three \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} (two fluid \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a200481dd99050de703e95310b8d7188a}{velocities}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} one \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a622e9a161fe300e2ba2f734430187e19}{pressure}}) \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} is used as \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} an F\+SI \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_abc882676ce6535f83eef31e4c8889d44}{problem}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} also involves additional \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aea1877bbfb3f4a1f7d7c64edba58d5f5}{dofs}} associated \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} solid mechanics (e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} two solid displacement components). This was done by informing \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} full-\/sized system to regard as \char`\"{}its own\char`\"{} when calling its \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a09ffc1a7d36a15270a2438aafabc3063}{c}} turn\+\_\+into\+\_\+subsidiary\+\_\+block\+\_\+preconditioner(...) function. This implies \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} remains unaware of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7005143667a7d93ac15567de99c9459d}{any}} compound \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} may have been formed \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} its master preconditioner. The functionality presented so far only allows us to associate \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aebbb04ad59c9c8f15ddfeb395e4b5ee4}{blocks}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary block preconditioner. It is therefore not possible (without further functionality \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a4b5cfadf429584e0826f6ca83f3298aa}{which}} we explain \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} this \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aee0b46a7944d413c53157110d1f7f4d7}{example}}) to use \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} subsidiary block \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} if \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} are \char`\"{}too fine-\/grained\char`\"{}. This arises, for \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acdb7a40a5c0efe5eff5bb57ba88d5b24}{instance}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} Navier-\/Stokes \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a585197cbf62aba1f1ec0bbb2b5c4c0c9}{problems}} where \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} master \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} sub-\/divides \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} two components of \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} fluid velocity into degrees of freedom on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} domain boundary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_acb2aec021f42d03f2963c9629bd28efb}{and}} those \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a1ebf85fa72491b7dec0b45191dc0c939}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} interior. It is then necessary to make \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} subsidiary \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a608311580f56d31827f06e0afcf45d9a}{preconditioner}} act on \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} combined \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a0229a9a76573f31c1a563ccbe15b5e8b}{dof}} \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aa2aff39dec31c93c43c6042c98753491}{types}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a7994473b56f803aacabc944c5e43c208}{a}} process \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} we describe as \char`\"{}coarsening\char`\"{}. We illustrate \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} procedure by returning, yet again, to our 5x5 block linear system \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ad49be126fe08dab1d4d0b8c180cc9e6c}{that}} we wish to precondition \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a2b6c7a2e8d2a64d9605b3058eab04e50}{with}} \textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_ae5d3b6fe51905f59612f7a9bf14caea4}{f}}\mbox{[} \textbackslash{}hspace\{3cm\} \{\textbackslash{}bf P\}\mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a18f05aeddc212b523b40818fa2b87b33}{\+\_\+}}\{\textbackslash{}rm previous\} = \textbackslash{}left( \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a193d0baa9ebd9824d79e8e7a441aea18}{However}}, now we wish to solve \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} two linear systems involving \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_a44f8d485630632af4bfa916579c9b880}{the}} compound subsidiary block preconditioner. acting on \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{block__preconditioners_8txt_aeb67b16f41be1903f840dc845012c7ec}{B\+\_\+}}\{22\}\textbackslash{}f\$ treats
